***reiziger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reiziger.html>reiziger</a> (13160)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">reisiger</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">reisiger</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soldier on horseback</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">reise</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">war expedition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reis.html>reis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">travel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reiziger.html>reiziger</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reizigers.html>reizigers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reiziger.html>reizigertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">traveller</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">voyager</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">endonym</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> Dutch people who live in <a href = vnd.unilang:wagons.html>wagons</a> or mobile homes, predominantly descended from 19th-century displaced agricultural workers
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamper.html>kamper</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:rekel.html>rekel</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. </p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rekel.html>rekel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rekels.html>rekels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rekeltje.html>rekeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***rekenen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rekenen.html>rekenen</a> (1906)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rēkenen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rekanon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rekanōną</i>, indirectly derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃reǵ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rekenen.html>rekenen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to calculate, to do arithmetic
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>Na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> taalles <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rekenen.html>rekenen</a></b>.</i>  |  <i>After the language lesson the children <b>do arithmetic</b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to count [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i> <span>(as (belonging to))</span></span>] [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a></i> <span>(as)</span></span>], to consider (something) an example [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i> <span>(of)</span></span>]
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rekende.html>rekende</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groten.html>groten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a>.</i>  |  <i>He <b> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a></b> already <b>counted</b> himself <b>as belonging</b> (to) the greats of the word/one of the greats.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to appraise, to reckon, to evaluate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rely [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(on)</span></span>], to depend [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(on)</span></span>]
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruiters.html>ruiters</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rekenden.html>rekenden</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:bijstand.html>bijstand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koning.html>koning</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:berg.html>berg</a>.</i>  |  <i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:riders.html>riders</a>/horsemen <b>counted</b> (on) the king's assistance under the mountain.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to charge, to determine or request a payment

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rekenen.html>rekenen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">calculate, do sums, reckon, count, charge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">recken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:rekken.html>rekken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*rakkjan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rakjaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stretch, to straighten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃roǵéyeti</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> relax (3028)</h1><br></body> 
***relaxed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:relaxed.html>relaxed</a> (15765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:relaxed.html>relaxed</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:relaxed.html>relaxed</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:relaxed.html>relaxed</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Having an easy-going mood or temperament.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He's a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:relaxed.html>relaxed</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of guy, he never <a href = vnd.unilang:lets.html>lets</a> himself get upset.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Eased or loosened.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:relaxed.html>relaxed</a></b> rules <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> greatly tightened after the lawsuit.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1898</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winston_Churchill_(novelist)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Winston Churchill (novelist)">Winston Churchill</a>,  chapter 8, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Celebrity" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Celebrity">The Celebrity</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I corralled the judge, and <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> started off across the fields, in no very mild state of fear of that gentleman's wife, whose vigilance <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> seldom <b><a href = vnd.unilang:relaxed.html>relaxed</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Free from tension or anxiety; at ease.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2019</b>,  Li Huang |  James <a href = vnd.unilang:lambert.html>Lambert</a>,  “Another Arrow for the Quiver: A New Methodology for Multilingual Researchers”, in  <cite>Journal of Multilingual and Multicultural Development</cite>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Digital_object_identifier" class="extiw" title="w:Digital object identifier">DOI</a>:<span class="neverexpand"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://doi.org/10.1080%2F01434632.2019.1596115">10.1080/01434632.2019.1596115</a></span></small>, page 4:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Students and faculty members <a href = vnd.unilang:lunch.html>lunch</a> at the cafeteria and naturally communicate freely with one another in a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:relaxed.html>relaxed</a></b> and informal setting.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">calm</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:relaxed.html>relaxed</a></strong>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brengend.html>brengend</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:relaxed.html>relaxed</a></b> peddeltochtje <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:barre.html>barre</a> overlevingstocht.</i> </li>

***religie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:religie.html>religie</a> (5965)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:religie.html>religie</a></i>, earlier also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">religioen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">religion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">religiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:religie.html>religie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:religies.html>religies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:religie.html>religietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> faith, religion, a system of beliefs dealing with soul, deity and/or life after death
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:overheid.html>overheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoort.html>hoort</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:religie.html>religie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedrijven.html>bedrijven</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A government shouldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> be in the business of managing <b>religion</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>religious denomination, such as an organized church</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> something one adheres to devotedly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:minuscuul.html>minuscuul</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:prentje.html>prentje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:zonnebloemen.html>Zonnebloemen</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> Gogh <a href = vnd.unilang:gaf.html>gaf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kennen.html>kennen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> ten <a href = vnd.unilang:huize.html>huize</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> sociaaldemocratie <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:religie.html>religie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A <a href = vnd.unilang:minuscule.html>minuscule</a> picture of <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> Gogh's <i>Sunflowers</i> indicated that social democracy <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the practiced <b>religion</b> here in our home.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">faith</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloof</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">denomination</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geloof.html>geloof</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">confessie</span></li></ul>

***remains.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a> (88824)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>What <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> left after a person (or any organism) <a href = vnd.unilang:dies.html>dies</a>; a corpse.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">They buried the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a></b> of their longtime friend in the town cemetery.</i></div></dd>
<dd><i>The victim's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> one small piece of bone.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Historical or archaeological relics.</li>
<li class="senseid" id="English-writings">The extant writings of a deceased person.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">To his great intellectual powers his published <b><a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a></b> bear abundant witness.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>All that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> left of the stock of some <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a>; remnants.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1963</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Margery_Allingham" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Margery Allingham">Margery Allingham</a>,  “Foreword”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_China_Governess" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The China Governess">The China Governess</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL2004261W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Everything a living animal could do to destroy and to desecrate <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> and walls <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> done. [ | ]  A canister of flour from the kitchen <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> thrown at the looking-glass and lay like trampled snow <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a></b> of a decent blue suit with the lining ripped out which lay on top of the ruin of a plastic wardrobe.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He couldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> bring himself to eat the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a></b> of the chicken dinner.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:remains.html>remains</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">remain</i></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:remt.html>remt</a> (25625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***rennen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rennen.html>rennen</a> (1018)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A merger of two related verbs:
</p>
<ul><li><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rinnen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flow, to run fast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rinnan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rinnaną</i>.</li>
<li><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:rennen.html>rennen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to run/ride fast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:rennen.html>rennen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rannijaną</i>.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rennen.html>rennen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> about people or animals</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run, to move fast</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> about fluids</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run, flow, stream</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> about fluids</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to flow together, combine, thicken</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leak, seep through</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:renner.html>renner</a> (16483)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rennen.html>rennen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to run</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***reppen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reppen.html>reppen</a> (53395)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:reppen.html>reppen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to set in motion, to touch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:reppen.html>reppen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrapjaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reppen.html>reppen</a></strong>
</p>

***reptiel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reptiel.html>reptiel</a> (16340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">reptile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">reptile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rēptile</i>, neuter of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">reptilis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">creeping</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rēpō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to creep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*rep-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to creep, <a href = vnd.unilang:slink.html>slink</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (Pokorny; Watkins, 1969).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reptiel.html>reptiel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reptielen.html>reptielen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reptieltje.html>reptieltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>reptile, any member of the class Reptilia
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kruipdier</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***requiem.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:requiem.html>requiem</a> (46567)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The first word of the introit for the traditional <a href = vnd.unilang:requiem.html>requiem</a> mass, an alternative accusative case of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">requiēs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a>, repose</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">re-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">again</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">quiēs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a>, quiet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:requiem.html>requiem</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">requiems</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A mass (especially Catholic) to honor and remember a dead person.</li>
<li>A musical composition for such a mass.</li>
<li>A piece of music composed to honor a dead person.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a>; peace</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:requiem.html>requiem</a> mass</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">requiescat</span></li>
<li>See related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> of quiet</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">requin</i>, altered by association with Etymology 1, above.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:requiem.html>requiem</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">requiems</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A large or dangerous shark, specifically, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a member of the family Carcharhinidae.
<ul><li><b>1973</b>, Patrick Buchanan, <i>A <a href = vnd.unilang:requiem.html>Requiem</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:sharks.html>Sharks</a></i>:
<dl><dd>Any man-eater <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:requiem.html>requiem</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
